				limit = {

				}

			else_if = {

	id = custom_difficulty_mm.22
	 #update newly created countries without having to open menu
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			country_event = { id = custom_difficulty_mm.20 }
		}
		else = { country_event = { id = custom_difficulty_mm.21 } }
	}
}
